# <a name="edifact-transaction-sets-aperak-iftrin"></a><span data-ttu-id="0f2db-102">EDIFACT 事务集 APERAK-IFTRIN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0f2db-102">EDIFACT Transaction Sets APERAK-IFTRIN</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="0f2db-103">本主题列出了 BizTalk Server 支持的 EDIFACT 事务集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0f2db-103">This topic lists the EDIFACT transaction sets that are supported by BizTalk Server.</span></span>  
  
 <span data-ttu-id="0f2db-104">本主题包含以下事务集：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0f2db-104">The following transaction sets are contained in this topic:</span></span>

-   [<span data-ttu-id="0f2db-106">事务集 BOPBNK CLASET</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0f2db-106">Transaction Sets BOPBNK-CLASET</span></span>](../core/edifact-transaction-sets-aperak-iftrin.md#bopbnk)  
  
-   [<span data-ttu-id="0f2db-107">事务集 CNTCND CONAPW</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0f2db-107">Transaction Sets CNTCND-CONAPW</span></span>](../core/edifact-transaction-sets-aperak-iftrin.md#cntcnd)  
  
-   [<span data-ttu-id="0f2db-108">事务集 CONDPV CONWQD</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0f2db-108">Transaction Sets CONDPV-CONWQD</span></span>](../core/edifact-transaction-sets-aperak-iftrin.md#condpv)  
  
-   [<span data-ttu-id="0f2db-109">事务集 COPARN CREMUL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0f2db-109">Transaction Sets COPARN-CREMUL</span></span>](../core/edifact-transaction-sets-aperak-iftrin.md#coparn)  
  
-   [<span data-ttu-id="0f2db-110">事务集 CUSCAR DEBREC</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0f2db-110">Transaction Sets CUSCAR-DEBREC</span></span>](../core/edifact-transaction-sets-aperak-iftrin.md#cuscar)  
  
-   [<span data-ttu-id="0f2db-111">事务集 DELFOR DOCADV</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0f2db-111">Transaction Sets DELFOR-DOCADV</span></span>](../core/edifact-transaction-sets-aperak-iftrin.md#delfor)

-   [<span data-ttu-id="0f2db-113">事务集 GENRAL IFTIAG</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0f2db-113">Transaction Sets GENRAL-IFTIAG</span></span>](../core/edifact-transaction-sets-aperak-iftrin.md#genral)
